<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">щипну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščipnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущипнуть.html>ущипну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščipnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ущи́пывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pinch <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with fingers or a beak</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щипать.html>щипа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ščipátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ущи́пывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uščípyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pinch off, to remove (a small amount) by pinching</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hurt <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">morally or mentally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***уязвить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уязвить.html>уязви́ть</a> (15292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:язвить.html>язви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jazvítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уязвить.html>уязви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ujazvítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уязвля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sting, to wound
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1872</b>,  Николай Семёнович <a href = vnd.unilang:лесок.html>Леско́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikolai_Leskov" class="extiw" title="w:Nikolai Leskov">Nikolai Semyonovich Leskov</a>),  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%A1%D0%BE%D0%B1%D0%BE%D1%80%D1%8F%D0%BD%D0%B5_(%D0%9B%D0%B5%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Соборяне (Лесков)">Соборяне</a></cite>, part 1, chapter 5 |  translated as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isabel_Florence_Hapgood" class="extiw" title="w:Isabel Florence Hapgood">Isabel Hapgood</a>, transl., <cite>The Cathedral Folk</cite>, London, 1924, page 88:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:однако.html>одна́ко</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сколь.html>сколь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничтожный.html>ничто́жным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почитать.html>почита́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уязвлённый.html>уязвлён</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́том</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ядовитый.html>ядови́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оса.html>осо́й</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Odnáko, skolʹ ni ničtóžnym sevó čelovéka i vse jevó mnénija počitáju, no <b>ujazvljón</b> jevó otvétom, kak jadovítoj osój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Nevertheless, insignificant as I consider this man and all his opinions to be, yet I am <b>stung</b> by his answer, as by a poisonous wasp.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уязвить.html>уязви́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ujazvítʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hurt smb's pride</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уязвить.html>уязви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ujazvítʹ</b> sámoje bolʹnóje mésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to touch/cut/wound to the quick</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***уяснить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уяснить.html>уясни́ть</a> (10998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ясни́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jasnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уяснить.html>уясни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ujasnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уясня́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to understand, to grasp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уяснить.html>уясни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ujasnítʹ</b> sebé položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">get the hang of the situation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***фабрика.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фабрика.html>фа́брика</a> (3372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fabrica</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фабрика.html>фа́брика</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fábrika</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фабрика.html>фа́брики</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фабрика.html>фа́брики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фабрика.html>фа́брик</a></b>)
</p>

***факел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:факел.html>фа́кел</a> (5984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fackel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">vackel</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">faccala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facula</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:факел.html>фа́кел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fákel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:факел.html>фа́кела</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:факел.html>фа́келы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:факел.html>фа́келов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>torch (stick with flame at one end)</li>
<li>jet, tongue, flare</li>
<li>flame body</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фактор.html>фа́ктор</a> (3047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактор.html>фа́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fáktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактор.html>фа́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактор.html>фа́кторы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактор.html>фа́кторов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>factor (significant influence)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> factor</li>
<li>factor, factotum, agent, broker (doer, maker)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фактура.html>факту́ра</a> (26013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">factūra</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактура.html>факту́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">faktúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактура.html>факту́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактура.html>факту́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактура.html>факту́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>invoice, bill; bill of parcels</li>
<li>texture; pattern</li></ol>

***фальшивить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фальшивить.html>фальши́вить</a> (28501)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фальшь.html>фальшь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">falʹšʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фальшивить.html>фальши́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">falʹšívitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сфальши́вить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sing or play (e.g. a musical instrument) out of tune</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be hypocritical</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>

</th>
